       python.django.security.injection.tainted-url-host.tainted-url-host       
          User data flows into the host portion of this manually-constructed    
  URL. This could allow an                                                      
          attacker to send data to their own server, potentially exposing       
  sensitive data such as                                                        
          cookies or authorization information sent with this request. They     
  could also probe internal                                                     
          servers or other resources that the server runnig this code can       
  access. (This is called                                                       
          server-side request forgery, or SSRF.) Do not allow arbitrary hosts.  
  Instead, create an                                                            
          allowlist for approved hosts hardcode the correct host.               
          Details: https://sg.run/oYz6                                          
                                                                                
          257┆ endpoint = 'https://' + endpoint
